# Comments for Question 4, LLM=DeepSeek V3-0324

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=6.0)
    The story attempts meaningful symbolism with the net representing entangled fears, but this metaphor feels heavy-handed rather than subtle. While there's a clear emotional arc from fear to liberation, the transformation happens too easily to create genuine impact. The ending aims for profundity but relies on telling rather than showing Lena's transformation. The theme of self-discovery exists but lacks the nuance and complexity needed for lasting resonance.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=8.7)
    The story achieves remarkable depth through its metaphorical framework—the dollhouse as a reflection of the protagonist's life choices, the maps that rewrite themselves mirroring his potential for change. The central theme of confronting one's past and finding redemption is powerfully conveyed through imagery rather than exposition. The final image of Elias walking "into the hush" provides a resonant conclusion that suggests both resolution and new beginning.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story effectively uses the lamp as both literal object and metaphor for illumination/understanding. The transformation of the monster into something "almost human" carries emotional weight, and the ending provides satisfying resolution while maintaining a sense of mystery. The theme of reconnection and remembrance emerges organically. The story skillfully shows rather than tells the emotional journey, particularly in moments like "his hands shook" revealing the spy's true feelings beneath his confident exterior.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.9)
    The story effectively uses the pressed pennies as both literal objects and metaphorical devices ("The truth is a pressed penny—flattened, reshaped, but still metal beneath"), creating layered meaning. The cosmic deception theme resonates throughout, culminating in the revelation that "the deception is the universe itself." The ending provides closure while maintaining mystery. However, the story occasionally tells rather than shows emotional states, and some dialogue exchanges feel slightly stilted. The central conflict between truth-seeker and guardians of knowledge creates compelling tension, though the resolution could be more impactful.

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=7.5)

However, the dialogue occasionally feels too on-the-nose ("We start by letting go of the endings we never wanted"), telling rather than showing the theme. The conflict resolution would benefit from more nuanced development rather than the somewhat convenient appearance of the tenant.
